2026-03-15T03:04:10.8550231Z  
2026-03-15T03:04:10.8552973Z The root cause is `FindMaxGroupMembers=0` throughout the spawn, even after joining the group—the vanilla recruit system calculates max members from STAT_RESPECT, which is zero. When `AddRecruitToGroup` tries to call `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup`, it fails due to the zero member limit and falls back to `AddFollower` instead. At frame 808 the RESCAN fires but `FindMaxGroupMembers` is still zero, so the `g_joinedViaAddFollower` retry never triggers.
2026-03-15T03:04:10.8554940Z 
2026-03-15T03:04:10.8557234Z By frame 928, the task is `STAND_STILL` with `g_joinedViaAddFollower` true, but `FindMaxGroupMembers` remains zero. The RESCAN takes the "already in group" branch and calls `AddRecruitToGroup` again, which just hits the "recruta ja no grupo slot=0" path. The fundamental issue is that vanilla won't allow any followers when respect is zero, so `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` returns early on the member limit check. Even after the `AddFollower` backup and calling `ComputeDefaultTasks` with GangFollower, the task doesn't stick because the group membership itself never properly establishes.
2026-03-15T03:04:10.8559613Z 
2026-03-15T03:04:10.8561454Z Looking at the sequence: the ped spawns and gets added to `m_apMembers[0]` via the backup, then `SetPedDecisionMakerTypeInGroup` and `ComputeDefaultTasks` run, followed by `TellGroupFollowWithRespect`. The GANG_SPAWN_AI animation plays through frame 921, but when it ends, the ped reverts to STAND_STILL instead of maintaining the GANG_FOLLOWER task. Checking the task slots at frame 928 shows all slots are empty, which means the task assignment never persisted through the animation cycle.
2026-03-15T03:04:10.8573021Z 
2026-03-15T03:04:10.8575216Z The issue seems to be that `TellGroupToStartFollowingPlayer` (called via `TellGroupFollowWithRespect`) fails to assign the follow task to the primary slot because `FindMaxGroupMembers` returns 0, even though `ComputeDefaultTasks` successfully sets up the GangFollower allocator type when called directly. The task gets lost when the spawn animation finishes, suggesting the animation or task system is clearing the assignment.

2026-03-15T03:14:16.6897049Z 
2026-03-15T03:14:16.6898897Z I'll set the boost to 1000.0f to ensure it's high enough. Since `FindMaxGroupMembers` gets called before the boost for diagnostics, I need to update the PRE_JOIN log accordingly. 2026-03-15T03:17:04.7711443Z copilot: Everything looks good. Now let me also think about one more improvement to the WRONG_DIR detection/periodic snap interaction:
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7712525Z 
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7713134Z When `g_wasWrongDir=true` (we're in WRONG_DIR state), the current code does:
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7713783Z ```cpp
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7714230Z if (IsCivicoMode(g_driveMode) && !g_isOffroad && !g_wasWrongDir)

2026-03-15T03:17:04.7715118Z     ++g_civicRoadSnapTimer ...
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7715510Z }
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7715771Z else
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7716037Z {
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7716384Z     g_civicRoadSnapTimer = 0;  // Reset snap timer
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7716885Z }
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7717138Z ```
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7717291Z 
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7717923Z This resets `g_civicRoadSnapTimer` to 0 when in WRONG_DIR. That means when WRONG_DIR ends, the snap timer starts from 0 again. 
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7718708Z 
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7720791Z The periodic snap and WRONG_DIR state can both trigger `JoinRoadSystem` on the same frame without issues—calling it twice is harmless. Now I need to verify that the re-tentativa `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` branch properly removed the `FindMaxGroupMembers() > 0` check.
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7722829Z 
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7725515Z Since we're now boosting respect before the primary call, if it succeeds, `g_joinedViaAddFollower` becomes false and the branch never executes. If it fails (unlikely), the `FindMaxGroupMembers() > 0` check inside the branch is redundant anyway since we'll boost again there. The condition is essentially a dead fallback, though keeping the check provides extra safety even if it's not strictly necessary. though the boost inside will override it).
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7728459Z 
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7729367Z Hmm, actually if `g_joinedViaAddFollower=true` even after the boost, we should retry unconditionally. Let me change the condition to just `g_joinedViaAddFollower`:
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7730451Z 
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7733081Z No wait, the re-tentativa path is inside `else if (g_joinedViaAddFollower && FindMaxGroupMembers() > 0)` - the `FindMaxGroupMembers() > 0` check is from before when we didn't boost. Now that we boost inside, the check is redundant. But keeping it doesn't cause bugs - it just means the re-tentativa only runs when respect naturally goes up. This is acceptable since the primary call (with boost) should always succeed.
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7735600Z 
2026-03-15T03:17:04.7738830Z Actually, with the new boost code that cranks respect to 1000 at spawn time, `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` should always work, so `g_joinedViaAddFollower` should never even get set and the AddFollower fallback shouldn't be needed. But if the boost somehow fails—maybe the function checks something beyond just group capacity—the AddFollower path is still there as a safety net. Now I should verify whether that SLOW_ZONE comment needs updating too.

This ensures the ped is properly registered in `CPedGroupIntelligence`, which makes `TellGroupFollowWithRespect` work correctly. Same boost applied to the re-tentativa path.
2026-03-15T03:18:26.1898687Z       
2026-03-15T03:18:26.1901116Z       2. **Fix AdaptiveSpeed for curves** (`grove_recruit_drive.cpp`): `FindSpeedMultiplierWithSpeedFromNodes(m_nStraightLineDistance)` is useless here because `m_nStraightLineDistance` is always 20 (constant minimum) in MISSION_43/34, so speedMult was always 1.0. Replaced with a heading-diff-based multiplier: |dH|≤0.3→full speed, 0.3-1.5→linear 1.0→0.5, >1.5→0.3 minimum. `targetHeading` is now computed before `AdaptiveSpeed` and passed as a parameter.
2026-03-15T03:18:26.1903038Z       
2026-03-15T03:18:26.1904375Z       3. **Fix WRONG_DIR close-range** (`grove_recruit_drive.cpp`): When WRONG_DIR starts at dist<30m in CIVICO mode, call `SetupDriveMode` to restart the autopilot (JoinRoadSystem + full mission reset). This gives MISSION_43 a fresh start when it decides to circle the block at close range. Also skip the periodic road snap when `g_wasWrongDir=true` to avoid snapping to a wrong-direction link.
2026-03-15T03:18:26.1905748Z       
2026-03-15T03:18:26.1906314Z       4. **Reduce ROAD_SNAP_INTERVAL** (`grove_recruit_config.h`): 300→180 frames (5s→3s). Updated related comments in drive.cpp.

2026-03-15T03:18:40.3336605Z     
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3337272Z     **O que é:** mod para GTA San Andreas (PC, versão 1.0 US) que substitui o comportamento
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3338376Z     "ímã" dos companheiros de gangue por **IA veicular real**. O recruta dirige por conta própria,
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3339388Z     segue o jogador em carro, navega no road-graph nativo do motor RenderWare, desvia de
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3340238Z     obstáculos e mantém distância de segurança.
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3340722Z     
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3341755Z     **Problema no jogo vanilla:** recrutas simplesmente teleportam ou correm em linha recta
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3343173Z     para o jogador — sem lógica de rua, sem desvio de carros, sem respeito ao trânsito.
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3344110Z     
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3344385Z     **Stack:**
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3345215Z     - **GTA SA 1.0 US** — executável original sem patches
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3346039Z     - **CLEO 4** — scripting via opcodes RenderWare nativos
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3346757Z     - **Sanny Builder 3** — compilador de scripts CLEO
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3347609Z     - **DK22Pac/plugin-sdk** — SDK C++ para criar ficheiros `.asi` (DLLs nativas)
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3348505Z     - **ASI Loader** — injector de DLLs no processo do jogo
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3349308Z     - **Visual Studio** — compilação do ASI (MSVC, Win32, Release/Debug)
2026-03-15T03:18:40.3350088Z     - **Repositório:** `Reinoso-Pilado/tentativa1` (GitHub)

2026-03-15T03:21:39.7754071Z copilot: Here is a summary of all changes made to address the reported issues:
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7754432Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7754503Z ---
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7754614Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7754694Z ## Changes Summary
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7755120Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7755346Z ### 1. Fix STAND_STILL at spawn (`grove_recruit_group.cpp` + `grove_recruit_config.h`)
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7755679Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7757796Z **Root cause:** `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` silently fails at the start of the game because `FindMaxGroupMembers()` returns 0 when `STAT_RESPECT=0`. The ped was only added via the `AddFollower` fallback, which doesn't register the ped in `CPedGroupIntelligence` — so `TellGroupFollowWithRespect` and `ComputeDefaultTasks` couldn't find it and did nothing, leaving the recruit with `STAND_STILL`.
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7759447Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7762097Z **Fix:** A transient `STAT_RESPECT` boost to `RESPECT_BOOST_LEVEL=1000` is applied immediately before `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` and restored within the same frame. This makes `FindMaxGroupMembers() > 0`, allowing the join to succeed and the ped to be properly registered in `CPedGroupIntelligence`. This is fundamentally different from the old failed `ActivateRespectBoost` (which was *persistent* across frames).
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7764156Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7764381Z ### 2. Fix curve speed reduction (`grove_recruit_drive.cpp` + `grove_recruit_config.h`)
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7764713Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7765822Z **Root cause:** `AdaptiveSpeed` used `FindSpeedMultiplierWithSpeedFromNodes(m_nStraightLineDistance)`, but `m_nStraightLineDistance` is always `20` (fixed minimum) in `MISSION_43`/`MISSION_34` escort missions — so the multiplier was always `1.0`, giving no slowdown in curves.
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7766799Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7767831Z **Fix:** Replaced with a heading-diff-based multiplier: `|dH| ≤ 0.3rad` → full speed; `0.3–1.5rad` → linearly from `1.0→0.5` (`CURVE_SPEED_REDUCTION`); `>1.5rad` → `0.3` minimum. `targetHeading` is now computed by `ApplyLaneAlignment` before being passed to `AdaptiveSpeed`.
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7768758Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7769015Z ### 3. Fix WRONG_DIR close-range recovery (`grove_recruit_drive.cpp` + `grove_recruit_config.h`)
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7769383Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7770076Z **Root cause:** When `MISSION_43` decides to circle the block at close range, the car goes in the wrong direction with no recovery mechanism. The periodic snap during WRONG_DIR made it worse by snapping to a wrong-direction link.
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7770851Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7771603Z **Fix:** When WRONG_DIR starts at `dist < WRONG_DIR_RECOVERY_DIST_M (30m)`, `SetupDriveMode` is called immediately to restart the autopilot (full `JoinCarWithRoadSystem` + mission reset). The periodic snap is skipped when `g_wasWrongDir=true`.
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7772651Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7772805Z ### 4. Reduce `ROAD_SNAP_INTERVAL` (`grove_recruit_config.h`)
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7773042Z 
2026-03-15T03:21:39.7773407Z `300` frames (5s) → `180` frames (3s). More frequent re-alignment with road nodes, less drift accumulation.

2026-03-15T03:22:13.7143956Z copilot: <pr_title>
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7144938Z fix: spawn STAND_STILL, curve speed, WRONG_DIR recovery, faster road snap

2026-03-15T03:22:13.7145783Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7145919Z <pr_description>
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7147414Z Three root-cause bugs blocked the recruit from working reliably in a car: it froze on spawn (STAND_STILL), drove at full speed through every curve, and got stuck going the wrong direction when close to the player with no recovery path.
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7148629Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7148800Z ## Fixes
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7148990Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7149589Z ### 1 — Spawn STAND_STILL (`grove_recruit_group.cpp`)
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7151395Z `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` calls `FindMaxGroupMembers()` internally; with `STAT_RESPECT=0` that function returns 0 → join fails silently → ped is never registered in `CPedGroupIntelligence` → `TellGroupFollowWithRespect` / `ComputeDefaultTasks` do nothing → STAND_STILL.
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7152608Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7153033Z Fix: apply a transient `STAT_RESPECT` boost (restored in the same frame, no HUD side-effect) wrapping every `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` call:
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7153628Z ```cpp
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7154037Z float boostNeeded = std::max(0.0f, RESPECT_BOOST_LEVEL - savedResp);  // RESPECT_BOOST_LEVEL = 1000
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7154593Z if (boostNeeded > 0.0f) CStats::IncrementStat(STAT_RESPECT,  boostNeeded);
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7154995Z player->MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup(g_recruit);
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7155374Z if (boostNeeded > 0.0f) CStats::IncrementStat(STAT_RESPECT, -boostNeeded);
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7155715Z ```
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7156612Z Distinguished from the old persistent `ActivateRespectBoost` (removed previously due to HUD/gameplay side-effects): this boost lives for one call.
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7157661Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7158262Z ### 2 — Curve speed never reduced (`AdaptiveSpeed` in `grove_recruit_drive.cpp`)
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7160338Z `FindSpeedMultiplierWithSpeedFromNodes(m_nStraightLineDistance)` always returns `1.0` because `m_nStraightLineDistance` is pinned to its minimum value (20) in MISSION_43/34 — making `AdaptiveSpeed` a no-op.
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7162012Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7164389Z Replaced with a heading-diff-based multiplier: `targetHeading` (from `ApplyLaneAlignment`) is now computed first and passed into `AdaptiveSpeed`; the multiplier interpolates linearly from `1.0` at `|ΔH| ≤ 0.3 rad` down to `0.5` at `1.5 rad`, then `0.3` in full WRONG_DIR. `CURVE_SPEED_REDUCTION = 0.5` is the named constant controlling depth.
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7166556Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7167013Z ### 3 — WRONG_DIR close-range no recovery (`ProcessDrivingAI`)
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7168525Z When `|ΔH| > WRONG_DIR_THRESHOLD_RAD` and `dist < WRONG_DIR_RECOVERY_DIST_M` (30 m), MISSION_43 was circling the block indefinitely. On WRONG_DIR start, `SetupDriveMode` is now called once (transition-gated via `g_wasWrongDir`) to re-snap the car to the road graph and restart the autopilot mission from the current position.
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7170140Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7170770Z Periodic road snap is suppressed while `g_wasWrongDir = true` — snapping during WRONG_DIR was locking the wrong-direction node and prolonging the condition.
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7171347Z 
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7171470Z ### 4 — Road snap interval
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7172234Z `ROAD_SNAP_INTERVAL` reduced from 300 → 180 frames (5 s → 3 s) for faster drift correction under normal driving.
2026-03-15T03:22:13.7172718Z </pr_description>
